</div>

No Description

- param:
checkAnswer - A flag that determines if the answer ID should be validated before fetching voters.
    Default is `false`. If `true`, the method checks if the answer ID exists in the list
    of answers and throws an error if not.

### AnonymousGuildStructure



<div className='*:border-b [&>*:last-child]:border-b-0'><div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">partnered</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

No Description



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">verified</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

If the guild is verified.

- link:
https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/guild#guild-object-guild-features

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">fetch</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"{ (mode?: \"rest\" | \"flow\" | undefined): Promise<Guild<\"cached\" | \"api\">>; (mode: \"cache\"): ReturnCache<Guild<\"cached\"> | undefined>; }"}</code>
</div>

Fetch guild on API



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">iconURL</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"(options?: CDNUrlOptions | undefined) => string | undefined"}</code>
</div>

iconURL gets the current guild icon.

- link:
https://discord.com/developers/docs/reference#image-formatting

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">splashURL</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"(options?: CDNUrlOptions | undefined) => string | undefined"}</code>
</div>

splashURL gets the current guild splash as a string.

- link:
https://discord.com/developers/docs/reference#image-formatting
- param:
options - Image options for the splash url.
- returns:
Splash url or void.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">bannerURL</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"(options?: CDNUrlOptions | undefined) => string | undefined"}</code>
</div>

bannerURL gets the current guild banner as a string.

- link:
https://discord.com/developers/docs/reference#image-formatting
- param:
options - Image options for the banner url.
- returns:
Banner url or void

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">shardId</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"number"}</code>
</div>

Shard ID of the guild.

- returns:
Shard ID or -1 if the client is not gateway based.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">shard</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Shard"}</code>
</div>

Shard of the guild.

- returns:
Shard or undefined, if the client is not gateway based always undefined.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">

### WebhookStructure



<div className='*:border-b [&>*:last-child]:border-b-0'><div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">user</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"User"}</code>
</div>

The user associated with the webhook, if applicable.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">sourceGuild</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Partial<AnonymousGuild>"}</code>
</div>

The source guild of the webhook, if applicable.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">messages</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"{ write: (payload: { body: Omit<RESTPostAPIWebhookWithTokenJSONBody, \"poll\" | \"components\" | \"embeds\"> & SendResolverProps; query?: RESTPostAPIWebhookWithTokenQuery | undefined; }) => Promise<...>; edit: (payload: { ...; }) => Promise<...>; delete: (messageId: string, reason?: string | undefined) => Promise<...>; }"}</code>
</div>

Methods related to interacting with messages through the webhook.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"{ (mode?: \"rest\" | \"flow\" | undefined): Promise<Guild<\"cached\" | \"api\"> | undefined>; (mode: \"cache\"): ReturnCache<Guild<\"cached\"> | undefined>; }"}</code>
</div>

Fetches the guild associated with the webhook.

- param:
force Whether to force fetching the guild even if it's already cached.
- returns:
A promise that resolves to the guild associated with the webhook, or undefined if not applicable.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">channel</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"{ (mode?: \"rest\" | \"flow\" | undefined): Promise<AllChannels>; (mode: \"cache\"): ReturnCache<AllChannels | undefined>; }"}</code>
</div>

Fetches the channel associated with the webhook.

- param:
force Whether to force fetching the channel even if it's already cached.
- returns:
A promise that resolves to the channel associated with the webhook, or undefined if not applicable.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">avatarURL</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"(options?: CDNUrlOptions | undefined) => string | null"}</code>
</div>

Retrieves the avatar URL of the webhook.

- param:
options The image options for the avatar.
- returns:
The avatar URL of the webhook, or null if no avatar is set.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">fetch</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"() => Promise<Webhook>"}</code>
</div>

Fetches the webhook data from the Discord API.

- returns:
A promise that resolves to the fetched webhook data.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">edit</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"(body: RESTPatchAPIWebhookJSONBody | RESTPatchAPIWebhookWithTokenJSONBody, reason?: string | undefined) => Promise<...>"}</code>
</div>

Edits the webhook.

- param:
reason The reason for editing the webhook.
- returns:
A promise that resolves when the webhook is successfully edited.

</div>

</div>

- param:
reason The reason for deleting the webhook.
- returns:
